[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA fuzzing session using LibFuzzer against the Wireshark NetBIOS dissector [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`handler_netbios`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m triggered an AddressSanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASan[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m heap-buffer-overflow. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow occurs in the function `dissect_netb_terminate_trace` within [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-netbios.c` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m726[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, where a single-byte write exceeds a [0m[1;36m17[0m[39m-byte heap [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation. The crash was reproducible with a minimal test case under the fuzzing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The crash report shows ASan detecting a one-byte write past the end of a heap [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer. The offending write is in `dissect_netb_terminate_trace`, called from [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_netbios`.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This is a classic heap-buffer-overflow: writing one byte beyond an allocated [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m17[0m[39m-byte region.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The buffer in question is allocated via `g_malloc` inside `dissect_netbios`.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • ASan’s shadow memory indicates the write occurs exactly at offset [0m[1;36m17[0m[39m of a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m17[0m[39m-byte allocation.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace passes through the normal dissector invocation flow [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`call_dissector_*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `epan/packet.c`, indicating the overflow happens during [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket parsing rather than in the fuzz harness itself.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzz harness parameters include `-[0m[33mmax_len[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m` and a variety of disabled [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocols, focusing test inputs solely on NetBIOS.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Affected Code Areas  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To gain a holistic view, investigators should examine:  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The allocation point in `dissect_netbios` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m1213[0m[39m in [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-netbios.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which determines the buffer size.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The implementation of `dissect_netb_terminate_trace` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m726[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically how indices or lengths are computed and used for writes.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Any surrounding logic that calculates the number of trace entries or [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters to append, ensuring bounds checks match the allocated buffer size.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue arose when the NetBIOS dissector in `packet-netbios.c` triggered [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man AddressSanitizer heap-buffer-overflow inside `dissect_netb_terminate_trace`. The[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer showed a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write just past a [0m[1;36m17[0m[39m-byte region allocated for a signature [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA patch attempt replaced the fixed-size allocation with a dynamic calculation of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`sig_len` [0m[1;39m([0m[39meither `NB_SIZE_HMAC` or `NB_SIZE_TMAC`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and allocated `sig_len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes for a hex-encoded string. The patch also adjusted the call to [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`proto_tree_add_item` to use the correct length.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRe-running the fuzzer with AddressSanitizer revealed that the overflow no longer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurs, but introduced a memory leak: the dynamically allocated `signature` buffer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m33[0m[39m bytes in the failing test[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is never freed.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer command [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`handler_netbios -[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m consistently [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreproduces a heap-buffer-overflow.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - ASan’s stack trace pins the overflow to `dissect_netb_terminate_trace` at line[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m726[0m[39m of `packet-netbios.c`.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write goes out of bounds of a [0m[1;36m17[0m[39m-byte heap allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35mg_malloc[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m+ [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating an under-sized buffer for the signature processing.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `packet-netbios.c`, around line [0m[1;36m690[0m[39m, an `int sig_len` is introduced.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code replaces the old branches  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mflag & [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       signature = [0m[1;35mg_malloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNB_SIZE_HMAC + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     else[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       signature = [0m[1;35mg_malloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNB_SIZE_TMAC + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     with  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     sig_len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mflag & [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? NB_SIZE_HMAC : NB_SIZE_TMAC;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     signature = [0m[1;35mg_malloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39msig_len * [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39msignature == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `proto_tree_add_item` call for the signature field was updated to use [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`sig_len` instead of a hard-coded `[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m`.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The conversion loop remains to iterate over the signature bytes, writing two [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhex characters per input byte plus a terminating NUL.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Result  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow is resolved; the fuzzer no longer aborts on a [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap-buffer-overflow at that site.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - However, LeakSanitizer reports a direct leak of [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m bytes in one object [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated in `dissect_netbios`, indicating that the newly allocated `signature` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer is not deallocated.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The leak trace shows the allocation site [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`g_malloc`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in `dissect_netbios`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut no corresponding free.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Areas for Further Investigation  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The lifetime and ownership of `signature` in `dissect_netb_terminate_trace`: [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhere and whether it should be freed or handed off to a container that will free [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit.  [0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The APIs around `proto_tree_add_item` and related tree-node management, to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetermine if and when dynamically allocated data attached to tree items must be [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreleased.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Surrounding code in `dissect_netbios` and any post-dissector cleanup routines [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto ensure all allocated memory is properly reclaimed.[0m                               [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe initial issue was an AddressSanitizer report of a heap-buffer-overflow in the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction `dissect_netb_terminate_trace` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min packet-netbios.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The overflow [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccurred because the code allocated a buffer of size `NB_SIZE_HMAC+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` or [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`NB_SIZE_TMAC+[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` for a signature field, but then treated it as a hex-encoded string[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mwriting two characters per byte[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, overrunning the allocation.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patch attempted to fix this by:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Introducing a `sig_len` variable to select `NB_SIZE_HMAC` or `NB_SIZE_TMAC` based[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon a flag.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allocating `sig_len*[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m` bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto hold hex encoding plus a NUL terminator[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Replacing the raw `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with `[0m[1;35mg_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Adjusting the call to `[0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to use `sig_len` instead of a fixed[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter applying the patch, LeakSanitizer detected a [0m[1;36m33[0m[39m-byte memory leak originating [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom a `[0m[1;35mg_malloc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in `dissect_netbios`, indicating that the newly allocated [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer is not always freed.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A fuzzing run on `handler_netbios` with libFuzzer triggered:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    **ERROR: AddressSanitizer: heap-buffer-overflow**  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    at `packet-netbios.[0m[1;92mc:726:22[0m[39m` inside `dissect_netb_terminate_trace`.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The sanitizer stack trace shows a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write just past the end of a [0m[1;36m17[0m[39m-byte [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion allocated for `signature`.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allocation site: `[0m[1;35mg_malloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNB_SIZE_HMAC + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` or `[0m[1;35mg_malloc[0m[1;39m([0m[39mNB_SIZE_TMAC + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`; [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite site: a loop converting each byte to two hex digits and a terminating NUL.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The problematic region corresponds to the loop writing more data than was [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocated.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt [0m[1;39m([0m[39min `epan/dissectors/packet-netbios.c` around line [0m[1;36m690[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m740[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Declare `int sig_len;`[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Compute `sig_len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mflag & [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? NB_SIZE_HMAC : NB_SIZE_TMAC;`[0m                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Keep the conversion loop unchanged, then call `[0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_string[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[39m, i - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch result:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
